8a3('bum): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po da ltar slob pa ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs

8a5('bum): ba yin/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis skyob pa yin/ sbyin pa'i pha
8a6('bum): rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ yang dag par spong ba rnams la
8a7('bum): pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ dbang po rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ stobs ram
8a8('bum): la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ 'phags pa'i la ba yan lag brgyad pa la mi dmigs
8b1('bum): pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yan/ bsam gtan rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ tshad med
8b2('bum): rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ rnam par thar pa rnams la mi dmig
8b3('bum): pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa
8b4('bum): dang / smon pa med pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ mngon par shes pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ ting nge 'dzin rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyi
8b5('bum): slob pa yin/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ mi 'jigs pa rna
8b6('bum): la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ so so yang dag par rig pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ byams pa chen po la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sgyus
8b7('bum): yin/ snying rje chen po la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin no// shA ra dwa ti'i bus gsol

314a1('bum): ma/ kun du sa b+hi nge dzin la gnas/ rab tu gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin la gnas/ rin chen mapa'i ting nge 'dzin la gnas/ chos dam pa'i phyag rgya'i ting nge 'dren la gnas/ chos
